# Investigation: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update in Istio

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8c9b973 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/istio--f8c9b973 (mirror of istio/istio)
**Task Type:** Deep Causal Chain (investigation only — no code fixes)

## Scenario

An Istio service mesh operator reports that updating a DestinationRule in their cluster **silently fails to propagate** to Envoy sidecars. Specifically, when they have multiple DestinationRules for the same host (e.g., one defining subsets, another defining traffic policy), updating one of them does not trigger an xDS push — the Envoy sidecar continues serving the **stale** cluster and route configuration.

The operator has two DestinationRules for `reviews.default.svc.cluster.local`:

**DR-1 (traffic policy):**
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3
kind: DestinationRule
metadata:
  name: reviews-traffic-policy
  namespace: default
spec:
  host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local
  trafficPolicy:
    connectionPool:
      tcp:
        maxConnections: 100
      http:
        h2UpgradePolicy: UPGRADE
```

**DR-2 (subsets):**
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3
kind: DestinationRule
metadata:
  name: reviews-subsets
  namespace: default
spec:
  host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local
  subsets:
    - name: v1
      labels:
        version: v1
    - name: v2
      labels:
        version: v2
```

When the operator updates `reviews-subsets` (e.g., adding a `v3` subset), the Envoy sidecar does **not** receive updated CDS/RDS config. Only restarting the pod picks up the change. Updating `reviews-traffic-policy` also has no effect.

Istio debug endpoint `GET /debug/config_dump` on the sidecar shows the old configuration even after the DestinationRule has been updated in the Kubernetes API server.

## Your Task

Investigate the root cause of why updating a merged DestinationRule fails to trigger an xDS push, and produce a report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:

1. **How Istio merges multiple DestinationRules for the same host** — specifically the `mergeDestinationRule()` function in `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` and how it combines subsets and traffic policies from multiple DRs into a single merged config
2. **How the merged DestinationRule loses identity metadata** — when two DRs are merged, only one DR's `config.Config` metadata (name/namespace) survives in the `consolidatedDestRules` structure. The metadata of contributing DRs is lost.
3. **How SidecarScope builds config dependencies** — the `AddConfigDependencies()` calls in `pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go` that register which config resources a proxy depends on. Specifically, how `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` and `ConvertToSidecarScope()` iterate over `destinationRules` and add `ConfigKey{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: dr.Name, Namespace: dr.Namespace}` for each DR
4. **The specific gap: only one DR's ConfigKey is registered** — because the merged DR has only one name/namespace, `AddConfigDependencies` registers only that one DR. The other contributing DR(s) are not tracked.
5. **How the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig** — when a config change event occurs, `pilot/pkg/xds/` calls `SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(configKey)` to decide if the proxy needs a push. If the updated DR is the one whose metadata was lost during merging, `DependsOnConfig` returns `false` and the push is **incorrectly skipped**.
6. **The relationship between PushContext.destinationRule() and the merge pipeline** — how `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` stores the `destinationRuleIndex` and how `destinationRule()` returns the merged config, obscuring the fact that multiple DRs contributed to it

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Specific file, function, and mechanism>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted>

<Ordered list: symptom → intermediate hops → root cause>

## Recommendation
<Fix strategy and diagnostic steps>
```

- Focus on how the DestinationRule merging in `destination_rule.go` interacts with dependency tracking in `sidecar.go` and push filtering in the xDS layer

Let me verify the investigation report was created properly:
60-assistanttool_useRead
61-usertool_resultRead
     1→# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update
     2→
     3→## Summary
     4→
     5→When multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.
     6→
     7→---
     8→
     9→## Root Cause
    10→
    11→The root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.
    12→
    13→### Mechanism
    14→
    15→1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)
    16→   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:
    17→     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`
    18→     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)
    19→     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)
    20→     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)
    21→   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.
 
... (truncated)

   374→     name: reviews-subsets
   375→     namespace: default
   376→   spec:
   377→     host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local
   378→     subsets:
   379→       - name: v1
   380→         labels:
   381→           version: v1

   383→   ```

   393→   ```bash
   394→   kubectl patch destinationrule reviews-subsets --type merge \
   395→     -p '{"spec":{"subsets":[{"name":"v1","labels":{"version":"v1"}},{"name":"v3","labels":{"version":"v3"}}]}}'
   396→   ```
   397→

66-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive investigation of the Istio stale DestinationRule configuration issue. Here's what I found:

## Investigation Summary

I've produced a detailed investigation report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md` that traces the root cause of why updating a merged DestinationRule fails to trigger an xDS push.

### Root Cause: Four-Step Failure Chain

1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)
   - When two DestinationRules target the same host, `mergeDestinationRule()` modifies the EXISTING DR's config object in-place
   - The NEW DR's `config.Config` object is never added to the list
   - Only the first DR's Name/Namespace metadata survives

2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`sidecar.go:219-227`)
   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over merged DRs and calls `AddConfigDependencies()`
   - Since only one DR's metadata exists, only ONE ConfigKey is registered
   - The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `configDependencies`

3. **Push Filter Checks Fail** (`sidecar.go:521-540`)
   - When a config update occurs for the second DR, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if its ConfigKey is in the map
   - The hash is NOT found because the second DR was never registered
   - `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`

4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`ads.go:688`)
   - `DefaultProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false` because `ConfigAffectsProxy()` returned `false`
   - The proxy receives no updated configuration
   - Changes persist until pod restart

### The Report Covers

✅ **How Istio merges multiple DestinationRules** - consolidation logic in `mergeDestinationRule()`  
✅ **Metadata loss mechanism** - why only one DR's Name/Namespace survives  
✅ **SidecarScope dependency tracking** - incomplete registration in `AddConfigDependenc
... (truncated)

This\\n95: \\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\\n96: \\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\\n97: \\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\\n98: \\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\\n99: \\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\\n100: \\t// destination rule.\\n101: \\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\\n102: \\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\\n103: \\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\\n104: \\t// be forwarded.\\n105: \\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\\n106: \\n107: \\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\\n108: \\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\\n109: \\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\\n110: \\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\\n111: \\n112: \\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\\n113: \\t// Istio configuration.\\n114: \\t//\\n115: \\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\\n116: \\tRootNamespace string\\n117: }\\n118: \\n119: // MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\\n120: func (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\\n121: \\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\\n122: \\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\\n123: \\t\\t\\\"version\\\":               sc.Version,\\n124: \\t\\t\\\"rootNamespace\\\":         sc.RootNamespace,\\n125: \\t\\t\\\"name\\\":                  sc.Name,\\n126: \\t\\t\\\"namespace\\\":             sc.Namespace,\\n127: \\t\\t\\\"outboundTrafficPolicy\\\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\\n128: \\t\\t\\\"services\\\":              sc.services,\\n129: \\t\\t\\\"sidecar\\\":               sc.Sidecar,\\n130: \\t\\t\\\"destinationRules\\\":      sc.destinationRules,\\n131: \\t}, \\\"\\\", \\\"  \\\")\\n132: }\\n133: \\n134: // IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\\n135: // networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\\n136: // optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\\n137: // services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\\n138: type IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\\n139: \\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\\n140: \\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\\n141: \\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\\n142: \\n143: \\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\\n144: \\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\\n145: \\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\\n146: \\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\\n147: \\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\\n148: \\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\\n149: \\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\\n150: \\tservices []*Service\\n151: \\n152: \\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\\n153: \\t// As with per listener services, this\\n154: \\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\\n155: \\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\\n156: \\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\\n157: \\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\\n158: \\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\\n159: \\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\\n160: \\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\\n161: \\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\\n162: \\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\\n163: \\tvirtualServices []config.Config\\n164: \\n165: \\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\\n166: }\\n167: \\n168: const defaultSidecar = \\\"default-sidecar\\\"\\n169: \\n170: // DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\\n171: // that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\\n172: // We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\\n173: func Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n261: // of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n262: // A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n263: // deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\n264: // to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\n265: // or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\n266: // scalability.\n267: //\n268: // Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\n269: // reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. This design assumes pilot\n270: // tracks all endpoints in the mesh and they fit in RAM - so limit is few M endpoints.\n271: // It is possible to split the endpoint tracking in future.\n272: type XDSUpdater interface {\n273: \t// EDSUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n274: \t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n275: \t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n276: \t// registry name.\n277: \tEDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n278: \n279: \t// EDSCacheUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n280: \t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n281: \t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n282: \t// registry name.\n283: \t// Note: the difference with `EDSUpdate` is that it only update the cache rather than requesting a push\n284: \tEDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n285: \n286: \t// SvcUpdate is called when a service definition is updated/deleted.\n287: \tSvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n288: \n289: \t// ConfigUpdate is called to notify the XDS server of config updates and request a push.\n290: \t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n291: \tConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n292: \n293: \t// ProxyUpdate is called to notify the XDS server to send a push to the specified proxy.\n294: \t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n295: \tProxyUpdate(clusterID cluster.ID, ip string)\n296: \n297: \t// RemoveShard removes all endpoints for the given shard key\n298: \tRemoveShard(shardKey ShardKey)\n299: }\n300: \n301: // shardRegistry is a simplified interface for registries that can produce a shard key\n302: type shardRegistry interface {\n303: \tCluster() cluster.ID\n304: \tProvider() provider.ID\n305: }\n306: \n307: func NewShardKey(cluster cluster.ID, provider provider.ID) ShardKey {\n308: \treturn ShardKey(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", cluster, provider))\n309: }\n310: \n311: // ShardKeyFromRegistry computes the shard key based on provider type and cluster id.\n312: func ShardKeyFromRegistry(instance shardRegistry) ShardKey {\n313: \treturn \n319: func (sk ShardKey) Cluster() cluster.ID {\n320: \tp := strings.Split(string(sk), \"/\")\n321: \tif len(p) < 1 {\n322: \t\treturn \"\"\n323: \t}\n324: \treturn cluster.ID(p[0])\n325: }\n326: \n327: // PushRequest defines a request to push to proxies\n328: // It is used to send updates to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.\n329: type PushRequest struct {\n330: \t// Full determines whether a full push is required or not. If false, an incremental update will be sent.\n331: \t// Incremental pushes:\n332: \t// * Do not recompute the push context\n333: \t// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)\n334: \t// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time\n335: \t// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. Generally, only EDS will set this, but\n336: \t// in the future SDS will as well.\n337: \tFull bool\n338: \n339: \t// ConfigsUpdated keeps track of configs that have changed.\n340: \t// This is used as an optimization to avoid unnecessary pushes to proxies that are scoped with a Sidecar.\n341: \t// If this is empty, then all proxies will get an update.\n342: \t// Otherwise only proxies depend on these configs will get an update.\n343: \t// The kind of resources are defined in pkg/config/schemas.\n344: \tConfigsUpdated map[ConfigKey]struct{}\n345: \n346: \t// Push stores the push context to use for the update. This may initially be nil, as we will\n347: \t// debounce changes before a PushContext is eventually created.\n348: \tPush *PushContext\n349: \n350: \t// Start represents the time a push was started. This represents the time of adding to the PushQueue.\n351: \t// Note that this does not include time spent debouncing.\n352: \tStart time.Time\n353: \n354: \t// Reason represents the reason for requesting a push. This should only be a fixed set of values,\n355: \t// to avoid unbounded cardinality in metrics. If this is not set, it may be automatically filled in later.\n356: \t// There should only be multiple reasons if the push request is the result of two distinct triggers, rather than\n357: \t// classifying a single trigger as having multiple reasons.\n358: \tReason []TriggerReason\n359: \n360: \t// Delta defines the resources that were added or removed as part of this push request.\n361: \t// This is set only on requests from the client which change the set of resources they (un)subscribe from.\n362: \tDelta ResourceDelta\n363: }\n364: \n365: // ResourceDelta records the difference in requested resources by an XDS client\n366: type ResourceDelta struct {\n367: \t// Subscribed indicates the client requested these additional resources\n368: \tSubscribed sets.Set\n369: \t// Unsubscribed indicates the client no longer requires these resources\n370: \tUnsubscribed sets.Set\n371: }\n372: \n373: func (rd ResourceDelta) IsEmpty() bool {\n374: \treturn len(rd.Subscribed) == 0 && len(rd.Unsubscribed) == 0\n375: }\n376: \n377: type TriggerReason string\n378: \n379: // If adding a new reason, update xds/monitoring.go:triggerMetric\n380: const (\n381: \t// EndpointUpdate describes a push triggered by an Endpoint change\n382: \tEndpointUpdate TriggerReason = \"endpoint\"\n383: \t// ConfigUpdate describes a push triggered by a config (generally and Istio CRD) change.\n384: \tConfigUpdate TriggerReason = \"config\"\n385: \t// ServiceUpdate describes a push triggered by a Service change\n386: \tServiceUpdate TriggerReason = \"service\"\n387: \t// ProxyUpdate describes a push triggered by a change to an individual proxy (such as label change)\n388: \tProxyUpdate TriggerReason = \"proxy\"\n389: \t// GlobalUpdate describes a push triggered by a change to global config, such as mesh config\n390: \tGlobalUpdate TriggerReason = \"global\"\n391: \t// UnknownTrigger describes a push triggered by an unknown reason\n392: \tUnknownTrigger TriggerReason = \"unknown\"\n393: \t// DebugTrigger describes a push triggered for debugging\n394: \tDebugTrigger TriggerReason = \"debug\"\n395: \t// SecretTrigger describes a push triggered for a Secret change\n396: \tSecretTrigger TriggerReason = \"secret\"\n397: \t// NetworksTrigger describes a push triggered for Networks change\n398: \tNetworksTrigger TriggerReason = \"networks\"\n399: \t// ProxyRequest describes a push triggered based on proxy request\n400: \tProxyRequest TriggerReason = \"proxyrequest\"\n401: \t// NamespaceUpdate describes a push triggered by a Namespace change\n402: \tNamespaceUpdate TriggerReason = \"namespace\"\n403: \t// ClusterUpdate describes a push triggered by a Cluster change\n404: \tClusterUpdate TriggerReason = \"cluster\"\n405: )\n406: \n407: // Merge two update requests together\n408: // Merge behaves similarly to a list append; usage should in the form `a = a.merge(b)`.\n409: // Importantly, Merge may decide to allocate a new PushRequest object or reuse the existing one - both\n410: // inputs should not be used after completion.\n411: func (pr *PushRequest) Merge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n412: \tif pr == nil {\n413: \t\treturn other\n414: \t}\n415: \tif other == nil {\n416: \t\treturn pr\n417: \t}\n418: \n419: \t// Keep the first (older) start time\n420: \n421: \t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n422: \tpr.Reason = append(pr.Reason, other.Reason...)\n423: \n424: \t// If either is full we need a full push\n425: \tpr.Full = pr.Full || other.Full\n426: \n427: \t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n428: \tif other.Push != nil {\n429: \t\tpr.Push = other.Push\n430: \t}\n431: \n432: \t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n433: \tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 || len(other.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 {\n434: \t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated = nil\n435: \t} else {\n436: \t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n437: \t\t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n438: \t\t}\n439: \t}\n440: \n441: \treturn pr\n442: }\n443: \n444: // CopyMerge two update requests together. Unlike Merge, this will not mutate either input.\n445: // This should be used when we are modifying a shared PushRequest (typically any time it's in the context\n446: // of a single proxy)\n447: func (pr *PushRequest) CopyMerge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n448: \tif pr == nil {\n449: \t\treturn other\n450: \t}\n451: \tif other == nil {\n452: \t\treturn pr\n453: \t}\n454: \n455: \tvar reason []TriggerReason\n456: \tif len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason) > 0 {\n457: \t\treason = make([]TriggerReason, 0, len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason))\n458: \t\treason = append(reason, pr.Reason...)\n459: \t\treason = append(reason, other.Reason...)\n460: \t}\n461: \tmerged := &PushRequest{\n462: \t\t// Keep the first (older) start time\n463: \t\tStart: pr.Start,\n464: \n465: \t\t// If either is full we need a full push\n466: \t\tFull: pr.Full || other.Full,\n467: \n468: \t\t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n469: \t\tPush: other.Push,\n470: \n471: \t\t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n472: \t\tReason: reason,\n473: \t}\n474: \n475: \t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n476: \tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 && len(other.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 {\n477: \t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated = make(map[ConfigKey]struct{}, len(pr.ConfigsUpdated)+len(other.ConfigsUpdated))\n478: \t\tfor conf := range pr.ConfigsUpdated {\n479: \t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n480: \t\t}\n481: \t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n482: \t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n483: \t\t}\n484: \t}\n485: \n486: \treturn merged\n487: }\n488: \n489: func (pr *PushRequest) PushReason() string {\n490: \tif len(pr.Reason) == 1 && pr.Reason[0] == ProxyRequest {\n491: \t\treturn \" request\"\n492: \t}\n493: \treturn \"\"\n494: }\n495: \n496: // ProxyPushStatus represents an event captured during config push to proxies.\n497: // It may contain additional message and the affected proxy.\n498: type ProxyPushStatus struct {\n499: \tProxy   string `json:\"proxy,omitempty\"`\n500: \tMessage string `json:\"message,omitempty\"`\n501: }\n502: \n503: // AddMetric will add an case to the metric.\n504: func (ps *PushContext) AddMetric(metric monitoring.Metric, key string, proxyID, msg string) {\n505: \tif ps == nil {\n506: \t\tlog.Infof(\"Metric without context %s %v %s\", key, proxyID, msg)\n507: \t\treturn\n508: \t}\n509: \tps.proxyStatusMutex.Lock()\n510: \tdefer ps.proxyStatusMutex.Unlock()\n511: \n512: \tmetricMap, f := ps.ProxyStatus[metric.Name()]\n513: \tif !f {\n514: \t\tmetricMap = map[string]ProxyPushStatus{}\n515: \t\tps.ProxyStatus[metric.Name()] = metricMap\n516: \t}\n517: \tev := ProxyPushStatus{Message: msg, Proxy: proxyID}\n518: \tmetricMap[key] = ev\n519: }\n520: \n521: var (\n522: \n523: \t// EndpointNoPod tracks endpoints without an associated pod. The SidecarScope object is a semi-processed view of the service\n907: // registry, and config state associated with the sidecar crd. The scope contains\n908: // a set of inbound and outbound listeners, services/configs per listener,\n909: // etc. The sidecar scopes are precomputed in the initSidecarContext\n910: // function based on the Sidecar API objects in each namespace. If there is\n911: // no sidecar api object, a default sidecarscope is assigned to the\n912: // namespace which enables connectivity to all services in the mesh.\n913: //\n914: // Callers can check if the sidecarScope is from user generated object or not\n915: // by checking the sidecarScope.Config field, that contains the user provided config\n916: func (ps *PushContext) getSidecarScope(proxy *Proxy, workloadLabels labels.Collection) *SidecarScope {\n917: \t// Find the most specific matching sidecar config from the proxy's\n918: \t// config namespace If none found, construct a sidecarConfig on the fly\n919: \t// that allows the sidecar to talk to any namespace (the default\n920: \t// behavior in the absence of sidecars).\n921: \tif sidecars, ok := ps.sidecarIndex.sidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]; ok {\n922: \t\t// TODO: logic to merge multiple sidecar resources\n923: \t\t// Currently we assume that there will be only one sidecar config for a namespace.\n924: \t\tif proxy.Type == Router {\n925: \t\t\tfor _, wrapper := range sidecars {\n926: \t\t\t\t// Gateways should just have a default scope with egress: */*\n927: \t\t\t\tif wrapper.Sidecar == nil {\n928: \t\t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n929: \t\t\t\t}\n930: \t\t\t}\n931: \t\t}\n932: \t\tif proxy.Type == SidecarProxy {\n933: \t\t\tfor _, wrapper := range sidecars {\n934: \t\t\t\tif wrapper.Sidecar != nil {\n935: \t\t\t\t\tsidecar := wrapper.Sidecar\n936: \t\t\t\t\t// if there is no workload selector, the config applies to all workloads\n937: \t\t\t\t\t// if there is a workload selector, check for matching workload labels\n938: \t\t\t\t\tif sidecar.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil {\n939: \t\t\t\t\t\tworkloadSelector := labels.Instance(sidecar.GetWorkloadSelector().GetLabels())\n940: \t\t\t\t\t\t// exclude workload selector that not match\n941: \t\t\t\t\t\tif !workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(workloadSelector) {\n942: \t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n943: \t\t\t\t\t\t}\n944: \t\t\t\t\t}\n945: \n946: \t\t\t\t\t// it is guaranteed sidecars with selectors are put in front\n947: \t\t\t\t\t// and the sidecars are sorted by creation timestamp,\n948: \t\t\t\t\t// return exact/wildcard matching one directly\n949: \t\t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n950: \t\t\t\t}\n951: \t\t\t\t// this happens at last, it is the default sidecar scope\n952: \t\t\t\treturn wrapper\n953: \t\t\t}\n954: \t\t}\n955: \t}\n956: \n957: \t// We didn't have a Sidecar in the namespace. This means we should use the default - either an implicit\n958: \t// default selecting everything, or pulling from the root namespace.\n959: \tps.sidecarIndex.defaultSidecarMu.Lock()\n960: \tdefer ps.sidecarIndex.defaultSidecarMu.Unlock()\n961: \tif proxy.Type == Router {\n962: \t\tsc, f := ps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]\n963: \t\tif f {\n964: \t\t\t// We have already computed the scope for this namespace, just fetch it\n965: \t\t\treturn sc\n966: \t\t}\n967: \t\tcomputed := DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n968: \t\tps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n969: \t\treturn computed\n970: \t}\n971: \tsc, f := ps.sidecarIndex.computedSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]\n972: \tif f {\n973: \t\t// We have already computed the scope for this namespace, just fetch it\n974: \t\treturn sc\n975: \t}\n976: \t// We need to compute this namespace\n977: \tvar computed *SidecarScope\n978: \tif ps.sidecarIndex.rootConfig != nil {\n979: \t\tcomputed = ConvertToSidecarScope(ps, ps.sidecarIndex.rootConfig, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n980: \t} else {\n981: \t\tcomputed = DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n982: \t\t// Even though we are a sidecar, we can store this as a gateway one since it could be used by a gateway\n983: \t\tps.sidecarIndex.gatewayDefaultSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n984: \t}\n985: \tps.sidecarIndex.computedSidecarsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] = computed\n986: \treturn computed\n987: }\n988: \n989: // destinationRule returns a destination rule for a service name in a given namespace.\n990: func (ps *PushContext) destinationRule(proxyNameSpace string, service *Service) []*config.Config {\n991: \tif service == nil {\n992: \t\treturn nil\n993: \t}\n994: \t// If the proxy config namespace is same as the root config namespace\n995: \t// look for dest rules in the service's namespace first. This hack is needed\n996: \t// because sometimes, istio-system tends to become the root config namespace.\n997: \t// Destination rules are defined here for global purposes. We do not want these\n998: \t// catch all destination rules to be the only dest rule, when processing CDS for\n999: \t// proxies like the istio-ingressgateway or istio-egressgateway.\n1000: \t// If there are no service specific dest rules, we will end up picking up the same\n1001: \t// rules anyway, later in the code\n1002: \n1003: \t// 1. select destination rule from proxy config namespace\n1004: \tif proxyNameSpace != ps.Mesh.RootNamespace {\n1005: \t\t// search through the DestinationRules in proxy's namespace first\n1006: \t\tif ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace] != nil {\n1007: \t\t\tif hostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(service.Hostname,\n1008: \t\t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules,\n1009: \t\t\t); ok {\n1010: \t\t\t\treturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules[hostname]\n1011: \t\t\t}\n1012: \t\t}\n1013: \t} else {\n1014: \t\t// If this is a namespace local DR in the same namespace, this must be meant for this proxy, so we do not\n1015: \t\t// need to worry about overriding other DRs with *.local type rules here. If we ignore this, then exportTo=. in\n1016: \t\t// root namespace would always be ignored\n1017: \t\tif hostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(service.Hostname,\n1018: \t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules,\n1019: \t\t); ok {\n1020: \t\t\treturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules[hostname]\n1021: \t\t}\n1022: \t}\n1023: \n1024: \t// 2. select destination rule from service namespace\n1025: \tsvcNs := service.Attributes.Namespace\n1026: \n1027: \t// This can happen when finding the subset labels for a proxy in root namespace.\n1028: \t// Because based on a pure cluster's fqdn, we do not know the service and\n1029: \t// construct a fake service without setting Attributes at all.\n1030: \tif svcNs == \"\" {\n1031: svc.Attributes.Namespace\n1034: \t\t\t\tbreak\n1035: \t\t\t}\n1036: \t\t}\n1037: \t}\n1038: \n1039: \t// 3. if no private/public rule matched in the calling proxy's namespace,\n1040: \t// check the target service's namespace for exported rules\n1041: \tif svcNs != \"\" {\n1042: \t\tif out := ps.getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(svcNs, service.Hostname, proxyNameSpace); out != nil {\n1043: \t\t\treturn out\n1044: \t\t}\n1045: \t}\n1046: \n1047: \t// 4. if no public/private rule in calling proxy's namespace matched, and no public rule in the\n1048: \t// target service's namespace matched, search for any exported destination rule in the config root namespace\n1049: \tif out := ps.getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(ps.Mesh.RootNamespace, service.Hostname, proxyNameSpace); out != nil {\n1050: \t\treturn out\n1051: \t}\n1052: \n1053: \t// 5. service DestinationRules were merged in SetDestinationRules, return mesh/namespace rules if present\n1054: \tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n1055: \t\t// return namespace rule if present\n1056: \t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[proxyNameSpace]; out != nil {\n1057: \t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n1058: \t\t}\n1059: \t\t// return mesh rule\n1060: \t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace]; out != nil {\n1061: \t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n1062: \t\t}\n1063: \t}\n1064: \n1065: \treturn nil\n1066: }\n1067: \n1068: func (ps *PushContext) getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(owningNamespace string, hostname host.Name, clientNamespace string) []*config.Config {\n1069: \tif ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace] != nil {\n1070: \t\tif specificHostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(hostname,\n1071: \t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].destRules,\n1072: \t\t); ok {\n1073: \t\t\t// Check if the dest rule for this host is actually nil\n1100: }\n1101: \n1102: // IsClusterLocal indicates whether the endpoints for the service should only be accessible to clients\n1103: // within the cluster.\n1104: func (ps *PushContext) InitContext will initialize the data structures used for code generation.\n1112: // This should be called before starting the push, from the thread creating\n1113: // the push context.\n1114: func (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) error {\n1115: \t// Acquire a lock to ensure we don't concurrently initialize the same PushContext.\n1116: \t// If this does happen, one thread will block then exit early from InitDone=true\n1117: \tps.initializeMutex.Lock()\n1118: \tdefer ps.initializeMutex.Unlock()\n1119: \tif ps.InitDone.Load() {\n1120: \t\treturn nil\n1121: \t}\n1122: \n1123: \tps.Mesh = env.Mesh()\n1124: \tps.LedgerVersion = env.Version()\n1125: \n1126: \t// Must be initialized first\n1127: \t// as initServiceRegistry/VirtualServices/Destrules\n1128: \t// use the default export map\n1129: \tps.initDefaultExportMaps()\n1130: \n1131: \t// create new or incremental update\n1132: \tif pushReq == nil || oldPushContext == nil || !oldPushContext.InitDone.Load() || len(pushReq.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 {\n1133: \t\tif err := ps.createNewContext(env); err != nil {\n1134: \t\t\treturn err\n1135: \t\t}\n1136: \t} else {\n1137: \t\tif err := ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq); err != nil {\n1138: \t\t\treturn err\n1139: \t\t}\n1140: \t}\n1141: \n1142: \tps.networkMgr = env.NetworkManager\n1143: \n1144: \tps.clusterLocalHosts = env.ClusterLocal().GetClusterLocalHosts()\n1145: \n1146: \tps.InitDone.Store(true)\n1147: \treturn nil\n1148: }\n1149: \n1150: func (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) error {\n1151: \tif err := ps.initServiceRegistry(env); err != nil {\n1152: \t\treturn err\n1153: \t}\n1154: \n1155: \tif err := ps.initKubernetesGateways(env); err != nil {\n1156: \t\treturn err\n1157: \t}\n1158: \n1159: \tif err := ps.initVirtualServices(env); err != nil {\n1160: \t\treturn err\n1161: \t}\n1162: \n1163: \tif err := ps.initDestinationRules(env); err != nil {\n1164: \t\treturn err\n1165: \t}\n1166: \n1167: \tif err := ps.initAuthnPolicies(env); err != nil {\n1168: \t\treturn err\n1169: \t}\n1170: \n1171: \tif err := ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env); err != nil {\n1172: \t\tauthzLog.Errorf(\"failed to initialize authorization policies: %v\", err)\n1173: \t\treturn err\n1174: \t}\n1175: \n1176: \tif := ps.initWasmPlugins(env); err != nil {\n1185: \t\treturn err\n1186: \t}\n1187: \n1188: \tif err := ps.initEnvoyFilters(env); err != nil {\n1189: \t\treturn err\n1190: \t}\n1191: \n1192: \tif err := ps.initGateways(env); err != nil {\n1193: \t\treturn err\n1194: \t}\n1195: \n1196: \t// Must be initialized in the end\n1197: \tif err := ps.initSidecarScopes(env); err != nil {\n1198: \t\treturn err\n1199: \t}\n1200: \treturn nil\n1201: }\n1202: \n1203: func (ps *PushContext) updateContext(\n1204: \tenv *Environment,\n1205: \toldPushContext *PushContext,\n1206: \tpushReq *PushRequest) error {\n1207: \tvar servicesChanged, virtualServicesChanged, destinationRulesChanged, gatewayChanged,\n1208: \t\tauthnChanged, authzChanged, envoyFiltersChanged, sidecarsChanged, telemetryChanged, gatewayAPIChanged,\n1209: \t\twasmPluginsChanged, proxyConfigsChanged bool\n1210: \n1211: \tfor conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n1212: \t\tswitch conf.Kind {\n1213: \t\tcase There may be multiple in some cases (especially multi cluster).\n2076: // * Warnings for references that could not be resolved. These are intended to be user facing.\n2077: func (gc GatewayContext) ResolveGatewayInstances(namespace string, gwsvcs []string, servers []*networking.Server) (internal, external, warns []string) {\n2078: \tports := map[int]struct{}{}\n2079: \tfor _, s := range servers {\n2080: \t\tports[int(s.Port.Number)] = struct{}{}\n2081: \t}\n2082: \tfoundInternal := sets.New()\n2083: \tfoundExternal :=   "content": "# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n\n### Mechanism\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n     ```go\n     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n     })\n     ```\n   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n\n3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n     ```go\n     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n     return exists\n     ```\n   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n\n4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n\n**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n            }\n```\n\n**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n```go\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add traffic policy if missing\n            if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n                mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n**Lines 101-104: New DR Config Is NOT Added**\n```go\n        if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {  // This is FALSE when merged\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n        }\n        return  // Exit without adding new DR's config\n    }\n```\n\n**Result**: The second DR's `config.Config` object (with Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\") is never stored.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Incomplete Dependency Registration (`sidecar.go:219-227`)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers only merged DRs:**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,         // Only MERGED DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,    // Only MERGED DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nSince `out.destinationRules` is populated from `ps.destinationRule()` (line 209), which returns only the merged config, only one DR's metadata is registered.\n\nSimilarly, lines 410-416 in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,      // Only MERGED DR\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. ConfigKey Hash Lookup (`config.go:60-74` and `sidecar.go:538`)\n\n**ConfigKey.HashCode() is based on Name, Namespace, and Kind:**\n```go\nfunc (key ConfigKey) HashCode() uint64 {\n    hash := md5.New()\n    for _, v := range []string{\n        key.Name,       // Different for \"reviews-subsets\" vs \"reviews-traffic-policy\"\n        key.Namespace,  // Same\n        key.Kind.Kind,  // Same (DestinationRule)\n        key.Kind.Group,\n        key.Kind.Version,\n    } {\n        hash.Write([]byte(v))\n    }\n    ...\n    return binary.BigEndian.Uint64(sum)\n}\n```\n\n**DependsOnConfig() checks for the hash:**\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    if sc == nil {\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists  // FALSE if \"reviews-subsets\" was never registered\n}\n```\n\nWhen `reviews-subsets` is updated, DependsOnConfig() is called with:\n```\nConfigKey{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}\n```\n\nIts hash is NOT in `configDependencies` because only \"reviews-traffic-policy\" was registered.\n\n---\n\n### 4. xDS Push Filtering (`proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `ads.go:688`)\n\n**checkProxyDependencies() calls DependsOnConfig():**\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {  // Returns FALSE\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE here\n}\n```\n\n**ConfigAffectsProxy() uses checkProxyDependencies():**\n```go\nfunc ConfigAffectsProxy(req *model.PushRequest, proxy *model.Proxy) bool {\n    for config := range req.ConfigsUpdated {\n        if affected && checkProxyDependencies(proxy, config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**DefaultProxyNeedsPush() checks ConfigAffectsProxy():**\n```go\nfunc DefaultProxyNeedsPush(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) bool {\n    if ConfigAffectsProxy(req, proxy) {  // Returns FALSE\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**ads.go:688 skips the push:**\n```go\nif !s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest) {\n    log.Debugf(\"Skipping push to %v, no updates required\", con.conID)\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        reportAllEvents(s.StatusReporter, con.conID, pushRequest.Push.LedgerVersion, nil)\n    }\n    return nil  // PUSH IS SKIPPED\n}\n```\n\nThe proxy receives no updated configuration and continues serving stale Envoy routes and clusters.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Consolidated Structure Hides Multiple DRs (`push_context.go:251-256`)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Map of hostname to LIST of configs\n}\n```\n\nWhile the structure supports multiple DRs per hostname (a list), the merging process ensures that:\n- For matching selectors, only ONE config object survives\n- The others' metadata is lost, making them \"invisible\" to dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`** - Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`** - Stores merged DRs in index, no tracking of contributing DRs\n3. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`** - Registers only merged DR's metadata in configDependencies\n4. **`pilot/pkg/model/config.go`** - ConfigKey hash depends on Name/Namespace\n5. **`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`** - Filters pushes using DependsOnConfig() check\n6. **`pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`** - Skips push if ProxyNeedsPush() returns false\n7. **`pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`** - Similar push filtering for incremental updates\n\n---\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n```\nStep 1: Multiple DestinationRules for same host are created\n        |\n        v\nStep 2: mergeDestinationRule() merges DR-2 into DR-1\n        - Modifies DR-1's config object in-place\n        - Sets addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n        - Does NOT add DR-2's config.Config to destRules[hostname] list\n        |\n        v\nStep 3: Only DR-1's metadata (Name, Namespace) is stored\n        - DR-2's metadata is completely lost\n        - p.destRules[hostname] = [DR-1 config only]\n        |\n        v\nStep 4: DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers config dependencies\n        - Iterates over ps.destinationRule() results\n        - Calls AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{Name: DR-1.Name, ...})\n        - DR-2's ConfigKey is never registered\n        |\n        v\nStep 5: User updates DR-2 (e.g., adds v3 subset)\n        - Config update event: ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-subsets\", ...}\n        |\n        v\nStep 6: xDS checks ConfigAffectsProxy() with DR-2's ConfigKey\n        - Calls checkProxyDependencies()\n        - Calls proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(DR-2's ConfigKey)\n        |\n        v\nStep 7: DependsOnConfig() computes DR-2's ConfigKey.HashCode()\n        - Looks up hash in sc.configDependencies map\n        - Hash NOT found (only DR-1's hash is there)\n        - Returns FALSE\n        |\n        v\nStep 8: checkProxyDependencies() returns FALSE\n        - ConfigAffectsProxy() returns FALSE\n        - DefaultProxyNeedsPush() returns FALSE\n        |\n        v\nStep 9: ads.go:688 skips the push\n        - if !s.ProxyNeedsPush(...) is TRUE\n        - return nil without pushing to proxy\n        |\n        v\nStep 10: Envoy sidecar receives NO updated configuration\n        - Continues serving stale routes and clusters\n        - Only a pod restart picks up the change\n```\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root issue is that **multiple contributing DRs lose their identity during merging**. To fix this:\n\n1. **Track All Contributing DRs**: Store the list of ALL contributing DR ConfigKeys in the `consolidatedDestRules` structure:\n   ```go\n   type consolidatedDestRules struct {\n       exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n       destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n       // NEW: Track ALL DRs that contributed to this merge\n       contributingConfigKeys map[host.Name][]ConfigKey\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Update mergeDestinationRule()** to record the ConfigKey of each incoming DR:\n   - When a merge occurs, append the incoming DR's ConfigKey to `contributingConfigKeys`\n   - When a new DR is added (no merge), record its ConfigKey\n\n3. **Update AddConfigDependencies()** in `sidecar.go`:\n   - Instead of only iterating `drList` (the merged config objects):\n     ```go\n     // OLD CODE: Only registers one DR per host\n     for _, dr := range drList {\n         out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{Name: dr.Name, ...})\n     }\n     ```\n   - Iterate ALL contributing ConfigKeys from the consolidatedDestRules:\n     ```go\n     // NEW CODE: Registers ALL contributing DRs\n     for _, cfg := range consolidatedDestRules.contributingConfigKeys[hostname] {\n         out.AddConfigDependencies(cfg)\n     }\n     ```\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo verify this issue in a cluster:\n\n1. Create two DestinationRules for the same host:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl apply -f - <<EOF\n   apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\n   kind: DestinationRule\n   metadata:\n     name: reviews-traffic-policy\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\n     trafficPolicy:\n       connectionPool:\n         tcp:\n           maxConnections: 100\n   ---\n   apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\n   kind: DestinationRule\n   metadata:\n     name: reviews-subsets\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\n     subsets:\n       - name: v1\n         labels:\n           version: v1\n   EOF\n   ```\n\n2. Check the sidecar's config dump:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl exec <pod> -c istio-proxy -- curl localhost:15000/config_dump | \\\n     jq '.configs[] | select(.type_url | contains(\"Cluster\"))' | \\\n     grep -A5 \"reviews\"\n   ```\n\n3. Update `reviews-subsets` to add a new subset:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl patch destinationrule reviews-subsets --type merge \\\n     -p '{\"spec\":{\"subsets\":[{\"name\":\"v1\",\"labels\":{\"version\":\"v1\"}},{\"name\":\"v3\",\"labels\":{\"version\":\"v3\"}}]}}'\n   ```\n\n4. Check the sidecar config again - it should update **immediately**. If it doesn't, the bug is present.\n\n5. Enable debug logging to observe the push filtering:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl port-forward -n istio-system svc/istiod 9881:9881\n   curl http://localhost:9881/debug/pprof/trace?seconds=5 > trace.out\n   # Look for calls to DependsOnConfig() returning false for \"reviews-subsets\"\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## Files and Line Numbers for Reference\n\n| Component | File | Lines | Purpose |\n|-----------|------|-------|---------|\n| Merge logic | `destination_rule.go` | 38-109 | Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata |\n| Consolidated structure | `push_context.go` | 251-256 | Stores merged DRs (line 255 has map) |\n| Merge calls | `push_context.go` | 1716, 1739, 1742 | Triggers mergeDestinationRule() |\n| Dependency registration (default) | `sidecar.go` | 219-227 | DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace registers DR deps |\n| Dependency registration (custom) | `sidecar.go` | 410-416 | ConvertToSidecarScope registers DR deps |\n| Dependency check | `sidecar.go` | 521-540 | DependsOnConfig checks if config affects proxy |\n| Config hash | `config.go` | 60-74 | ConfigKey.HashCode() based on Name/Namespace |\n| Proxy dependency check | `proxy_dependencies.go` | 60-74 | checkProxyDependencies calls DependsOnConfig |\n| xDS push filtering | `ads.go` | 688 | Skips push if ProxyNeedsPush returns false |\n| Similar filtering | `delta.go` | 141 | Incremental updates also skip based on ProxyNeedsPush |\n\n",

  "content": "# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.\n\n### Mechanism\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:\n     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`\n     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)\n     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)\n     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)\n   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.\n\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)\n   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` results\n   - For each returned DR, it calls:\n     ```go\n     out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n         Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n         Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the MERGED DR's name\n         Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the MERGED DR's namespace\n     })\n     ```\n   - Since `ps.destinationRule()` returns only one `config.Config` per hostname (the merged one), only ONE ConfigKey is registered.\n   - **Result**: The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `sc.configDependencies`.\n\n3. **Push Filter Skips Unknown ConfigKeys** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`)\n   - When a config update occurs, `DependsOnConfig()` checks if the proxy depends on that config:\n     ```go\n     _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n     return exists\n     ```\n   - The HashCode is based on Kind, Name, and Namespace (lines 60-74 in `pilot/pkg/model/config.go`)\n   - If the updated DR's ConfigKey hash is NOT in the map, `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`.\n\n4. **xDS Push Is Skipped** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74` and `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:688`)\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` (line 64)\n   - If it returns `false`, the push is filtered out\n   - At line 688 of `ads.go`, if `ProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false`, the push to the proxy is **skipped entirely**\n   - The proxy receives no updated xDS configuration and continues serving stale routes/clusters\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merge Function Loses Metadata (`destination_rule.go:38-109`)\n\n**Line 38-60: Merge Detection and Decision**\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, ...) {\n    rule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    resolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            bothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n            bothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n            selectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n            if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n                addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false  // LINE 60: Don't add new DR\n            }\n```\n\n**Lines 63-93: Merge Data Into Existing Config**\n```go\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy the EXISTING config\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n            // Add subsets from new rule to existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add traffic policy if missing\n            if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n                mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n**Lines 101-104: New DR Config Is NOT Added**\n```go\n        if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {  // This is FALSE when merged\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n        }\n        return  // Exit without adding new DR's config\n    }\n```\n\n**Result**: The second DR's `config.Config` object (with Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\") is never stored.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Incomplete Dependency Registration (`sidecar.go:219-227`)\n\n**DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers only merged DRs:**\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,         // Only MERGED DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,    // Only MERGED DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nSince `out.destinationRules` is populated from `ps.destinationRule()` (line 209), which returns only the merged config, only one DR's metadata is registered.\n\nSimilarly, lines 410-416 in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,      // Only MERGED DR\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false  // Returns FALSE ConfigAffectsProxy():**\n```go\nfunc DefaultProxyNeedsPush(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) bool {\n    if ConfigAffectsProxy(req, proxy) {  // Returns FALSE\n        return true\n    }\n    ...\n    return false  // Returns FALSE\n}\n```\n\n**ads.go:688 skips the push:**\n```go\nif !s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest) {\n    log.Debugf(\"Skipping push to %v, no updates required\", con.conID)\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        reportAllEvents(s.StatusReporter, con.conID, pushRequest.Push.LedgerVersion, nil)\n    }\n    return nil  // PUSH IS SKIPPED\n}\n```\n\nThe proxy receives no updated configuration and continues serving stale Envoy routes and clusters.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Consolidated Structure Hides Multiple DRs (`push_context.go:251-256`)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Map of hostname to LIST of configs\n}\n```\n\nWhile the structure supports multiple DRs per hostname (a list), the merging process ensures that:\n- For matching selectors, only ONE config object survives\n- The others' metadata is lost, making them \"invisible\" to dependency tracking\n\n---\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`** - Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`** - Stores merged DRs in index, no tracking of contributing DRs\n3. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`** - Registers only merged DR's metadata in configDependencies\n4. **`pilot/pkg/model/config.go`** - ConfigKey hash depends on Name/Namespace\n5. **`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`** - Filters pushes using DependsOnConfig() check\n6. **`pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`** - Skips push if ProxyNeedsPush() returns false\n7. **`pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`** - Similar push filtering for incremental updates\n\n---\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n```\nStep 1: Multiple DestinationRules for same host are created\n        |\n        v\nStep 2: mergeDestinationRule() merges DR-2 into DR-1\n        - Modifies DR-1's config object in-place\n        - Sets addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n        - Does NOT add DR-2's config.Config to destRules[hostname] list\n        |\n        v\nStep 3: Only DR-1's metadata (Name, Namespace) is stored\n        - DR-2's metadata is completely lost\n        - p.destRules[hostname] = [DR-1 config only]\n        |\n        v\nStep 4: DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace() registers config dependencies\n        - Iterates over ps.destinationRule() results\n        - Calls AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{Name: DR-1.Name, ...})\n        - DR-2's ConfigKey is never registered\n        |\n        v\nStep 5: User updates DR-2 (e.g., adds v3 subset)\n        - Config update event: ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-subsets\", ...}\n        |\n        v\nStep 6: xDS checks ConfigAffectsProxy() with DR-2's ConfigKey\n        - Calls checkProxyDependencies()\n        - Calls proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(DR-2's ConfigKey)\n        |\n        v\nStep 7: DependsOnConfig() computes DR-2's ConfigKey.HashCode()\n        - Looks up hash in sc.configDependencies map\n        - Hash NOT found (only DR-1's hash is there)\n        - Returns FALSE\n        |\n        v\nStep 8: checkProxyDependencies() returns FALSE\n        - ConfigAffectsProxy() returns FALSE\n        - DefaultProxyNeedsPush() returns FALSE\n        |\n        v\nStep 9: ads.go:688 skips the push\n        - if !s.ProxyNeedsPush(...) is TRUE\n        - return nil without pushing to proxy\n        |\n        v\nStep 10: Envoy sidecar receives NO updated configuration\n        - Continues serving stale routes and clusters\n        - Only a pod restart picks up the change\n```\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root issue is that **multiple contributing DRs lose their identity during merging**. To fix this:\n\n1. **Track All Contributing DRs**: Store the list of ALL contributing DR ConfigKeys in the `consolidatedDestRules` structure:\n   ```go\n   type consolidatedDestRules struct {\n       exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n       destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n       // NEW: Track ALL DRs that contributed to this merge\n       contributingConfigKeys map[host.Name][]ConfigKey\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Update mergeDestinationRule()** to record the ConfigKey of each incoming DR:\n   - When a merge occurs, append the incoming DR's ConfigKey to `contributingConfigKeys`\n   - When a new DR is added (no merge), record its ConfigKey\n\n3. **Update AddConfigDependencies()** in `sidecar.go`:\n   - Instead of only iterating `drList` (the merged config objects):\n     ```go\n     // OLD CODE: Only registers one DR per host\n     for _, dr := range drList {\n         out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{Name: dr.Name, ...})\n     }\n     ```\n   - Iterate ALL contributing ConfigKeys from the consolidatedDestRules:\n     ```go\n     // NEW CODE: Registers ALL contributing DRs\n     for _, cfg := range consolidatedDestRules.contributingConfigKeys[hostname] {\n         out.AddConfigDependencies(cfg)\n     }\n     ```\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo verify this issue in a cluster:\n\n1. Create two DestinationRules for the same host:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl apply -f - <<EOF\n   apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\n   kind: DestinationRule\n   metadata:\n     name: reviews-traffic-policy\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\n     trafficPolicy:\n       connectionPool:\n         tcp:\n           maxConnections: 100\n   ---\n   apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\n   kind: DestinationRule\n   metadata:\n     name: reviews-subsets\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     host: reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\n     subsets:\n       - name: v1\n         labels:\n           version: v1\n   EOF\n   ```\n\n2. Check the sidecar's config dump:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl exec <pod> -c istio-proxy -- curl localhost:15000/config_dump | \\\n     jq '.configs[] | select(.type_url | contains(\"Cluster\"))' | \\\n     grep -A5 \"reviews\"\n   ```\n\n3. Update `reviews-subsets` to add a new subset:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl patch destinationrule reviews-subsets --type merge \\\n     -p '{\"spec\":{\"subsets\":[{\"name\":\"v1\",\"labels\":{\"version\":\"v1\"}},{\"name\":\"v3\",\"labels\":{\"version\":\"v3\"}}]}}'\n   ```\n\n4. Check the sidecar config again - it should update **immediately**. If it doesn't, the bug is present.\n\n5. Enable debug logging to observe the push filtering:\n   ```bash\n   kubectl port-forward -n istio-system svc/istiod 9881:9881\n   curl http://localhost:9881/debug/pprof/trace?seconds=5 > trace.out\n   # Look for calls to DependsOnConfig() returning false for \"reviews-subsets\"\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## Files and Line Numbers for Reference\n\n| Component | File | Lines | Purpose |\n|-----------|------|-------|---------|\n| Merge logic | `destination_rule.go` | 38-109 | Merges multiple DRs, loses metadata |\n| Consolidated structure | `push_context.go` | 251-256 | Stores merged DRs (line 255 has map) |\n| Merge calls | `push_context.go` | 1716, 1739, 1742 | Triggers mergeDestinationRule() |\n| Dependency registration (default) | `sidecar.go` | 219-227 | DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace registers DR deps |\n| Dependency registration (custom) | `sidecar.go` | 410-416 | ConvertToSidecarScope registers DR deps |\n| Dependency check | `sidecar.go` | 521-540 | DependsOnConfig checks if config affects proxy |\n| Config hash | `config.go` | 60-74 | ConfigKey.HashCode() based on Name/Namespace |\n| Proxy dependency check | `proxy_dependencies.go` | 60-74 | checkProxyDependencies calls DependsOnConfig |\n| xDS push filtering | `ads.go` | 688 | Skips push if ProxyNeedsPush returns false |\n| Similar filtering | `delta.go` | 141 | Incremental updates also skip based on ProxyNeedsPush |\n\n",

# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update

## Summary

When multiple DestinationRules (DRs) target the same host, Istio merges them into a single consolidated configuration during PushContext initialization. The merging process **loses the metadata identity (Name/Namespace) of contributing DRs**, causing only one DR's ConfigKey to be registered in the SidecarScope's config dependencies. When a non-primary DR is updated, the xDS push filter uses DependsOnConfig() to check if the proxy is affected, but the check fails because the updated DR's ConfigKey was never registered. As a result, the xDS push is **silently skipped**, and the Envoy sidecar receives no updated configuration until the pod is restarted.

---

## Root Cause

The root cause is the **loss of metadata identity during DestinationRule merging**, combined with **incomplete dependency tracking** and **incorrect xDS push filtering**.

### Mechanism

1. **Metadata Loss During Merge** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`)
   - The `mergeDestinationRule()` function merges multiple DRs for the same host by:
     - Finding the existing DR in `p.destRules[hostname]`
     - Modifying the EXISTING DR's config object in-place (subsets, traffic policies)
     - If selectors match, setting `addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false` (line 60)
     - NOT appending the new DR's config to the list (line 102 is skipped when `addRuleToProcessedDestRules == false`)
   - **Result**: Only the first DR's `config.Config` object survives in `p.destRules[hostname]`. The second (and subsequent) DR's Name/Namespace metadata is **never stored**.

2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`)
   - `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` iterates over `ps.destina
... (truncated)
